                       <li data-reactid="1499"><p data-reactid="1500">The property at 3405 Bentonville is within 10 minutes from Conway's local box stores and grocery stores. The mobile home sits on a residential mobile home lot. The lots are small and trailers are close to one another. The front yard is mostly an unfenced side yard. It sits on a corner lot and is very close to the narrow streets. The mobile home is nice, clean and open and consists of three bedrooms and two baths. Kitchen is a nice size. All that is missing is a microwave and washer/dryer. We really missed a microwave. There is minimal cookware and dishes. The bathrooms had only a set of towels for each so be sure to bring your own. One TV in the living area that is a nice size. We had to turn it off and back on a few times because the sound would become garbled. Turning it off and back on would resolve the issue until it started again. There is cable and WiFi on premises. This property is for sale and the host is the realtor who wanted to show the property twice during our 9 day stay. </p><span data-reactid="1501">Deena</span><span data-reactid="1502">2017-03-30T00:00:00Z</span></li>

                    <div class="listingDescription_1woxt0o" data-reactid="2160">
                     <div data-reactid="2161">
                      <div data-reactid="2162">
                       It is all about the view. This chalet style house with floor to ceiling windows, has more than 180 degrees view of the lake, and sits 600 feet above the water. Don't be alarmed if a plane flies below you while you're sitting on the deck! A hot tub view from the deck is also available all year round. In our opinion, both the house and the lot make the view the best one in Diamond Bluff Estates!
                      </div>
                      <div data-reactid="2163">
                       The house faces north, and so the deck is largely in the shade and enjoyable, even in summer. There's almost always a gentle breeze to keep bugs from bugging you as well. We have outdoor dining set for 8, as well as 1 double and 1 single lounge plus two fatboys to jump into. A gas grill is also available (propane provided). Inside, three large bedrooms, all with full en suites provide privacy. An extra half back is located off the kitchen. Pool, ping-pong, and cards can all be enjoyed in the basement, that also has crazy views. Full sized, new laundry machines are located on the main floor. The main floor open plan kitchen, dining and living room allow family participation over a large area, with a TV and a projector, beautiful views and outdoor access. 22 ft ceilings! The lake is a "picture portrait" through the huge 9ft windows - the comfortable sectional seating makes lounging, reading, napping and TV watching (42" HD TV -Direct TV) all enjoyable, and a wood fireplace completes the room. Enjoy cooking meals in the large kitchen which features a double door refrigerator (ice maker and water dispenser), gas stove with double oven, microwave, dishwasher, drip coffee maker, espresso machine, and toaster. The kitchen is fully stocked with glass and plastic dinner sets, silverware, pots, pans, casserole dishes, a panini grill and a blender. There is an additional drink (wine) cooler in the basement. The Master bedroom on the main level has an en suite bathroom, modern glass and tile shower. It features a king bed, with a door to the deck with great views of the lake. The view at night with full moon is just amazing! The 2nd and 3rd bedrooms are in the basement and each have newly remodeled generous en suite bathrooms. Again the views are spectacular in every room. The 2nd bedroom has another king size bed and en suite bathroom as well as a built in closets. The 3rd bedroom has also an en suite bathroom, that is newly remodeled with frame less glass and a modern vanity. The bedroom has two bunk beds - each with a double on the bottom and single on the top. There are also drawers and space to hang clothes. The lower level common room features a ping pong/pool table. There is a wine cooler, and high backed bar stools for socializing and relaxing. A set of binoculars allows guests to watch the birds (including Bald Eagles), chipmunks, rabbits and occasional deer. The house is located in a dry county. There are several restaurants nearby. Boat launch is 5 minutes from the house, which is what we do every time we get on the water. Otherwise, the nearest marina is 12 minutes away.
                      </div>
